fx = 1000
#------------------------ Début dichotomie -------------------------

#Pour ce support le frottement est suivant X
from Utilitai.Osup import SharedVar as sv
ratioPlatine = RatioPlatine(value) 
reportFile = open(resultfile,"w")
reportFile.write(f'{version}\n{dash}')
reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX={fx}, FY = 0, FZ = 0\n')
reportFile.close()
force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
	FX = fx,),
);
stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
		_F(CHARGE=force,),
    ),
SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11),
);
stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
	MODELE=model,
	CHAM_MATER=material,
	CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
	RESULTAT = stat,
	CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
);
TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
	GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
	TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
	OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
    
contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
Sn = contrainte.SN
Svy = contrainte.SVY
Svz = contrainte.SVZ
Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
Smt = contrainte.SMT
 
ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);
#----------------------Borne max FX------------------------------
a1 = 0

while ratioMax < ratioLimProf:

#----------------------------------QUADRANT 1 FX >0 , FY > 0-------------------------------
for i in range(1,n):
    fy = fyMax/n*i    
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fzMax,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzMax),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),

        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',

    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
    Smt = contrainte.SMT

    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);    
    if ratioMax < ratioLimProf:
        fzMax *= 2
    fzCourbe = -fzMax/fyMax*fy + fzMax
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fzCourbe,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzCourbe),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
    );
    TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
    contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
    Sn = contrainte.SN
    Svy = contrainte.SVY
    Svz = contrainte.SVZ
    Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
    Smt = contrainte.SMT
    ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
    ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);    
    if ratioMax > ratioLimProf:
        alpha = 0
        beta = fzCourbe
    else:
        alpha = fzCourbe
        beta = fzMax
    fz = (alpha + beta)/2
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX ={round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fz,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,FZ=fz,FY=fy),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),

        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',

        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);

    Svz = contrainte.SVZ
    Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
    Smt = contrainte.SMT

    ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);
    while abs((ratioLimProf-0.01)-ratioMax) > 0.01:
        if ratioMax < ratioLimProf:
            alpha = fz
        else:
            beta = fz
        fz = (alpha+beta)/2
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fz,2)}\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,FZ=fz,FY=fy),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
            MODELE=model,
            CHAM_MATER=material,
            CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            RESULTAT = stat,
            CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
        );
        TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
            
        contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
        Sn = contrainte.SN
        Svy = contrainte.SVY
        Svz = contrainte.SVZ
        Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
        Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
        Smt = contrainte.SMT
        ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
        ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);
    #-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    ratio.writeOsupFile(curveFile, f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5, fy, fz)
    sv.fxCourbeMin.append(fy)
    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fz)
osupFile = open(curveFile,"a")
osupFile.write(f'{round(f*fyMax,2)}		{round(fyMax,2)}		0\n')
osupFile.close()
sv.fxCourbeMin.append(fyMax)
sv.fzCourbeMin.append(0)

for i in range(1,n):

    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzMin**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fzMin,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()

    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),

    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);

    if ratioMax < ratioLimProf:
        fzMin *= 2
    fzCourbe = fzMin/fyMax*fy + fzMin
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fzCourbe,2)}\n')

    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzCourbe),
    );

    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );

    Svz = contrainte.SVZ

    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ

    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);    
    if ratioMax > ratioLimProf:
        alpha = 0
        beta = fzCourbe
    else:
        alpha = fzCourbe
        beta = -fzMax
    fz = (alpha + beta)/2
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX ={round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fz,2)}\n')

        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );

    while abs((ratioLimProf-0.01)-ratioMax) > 0.01:
        if ratioMax < ratioLimProf:
            alpha = fz

            beta = fz
        fz = (alpha+beta)/2
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")

    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzMax),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
    );
    TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
    contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
    Sn = contrainte.SN
    Svy = contrainte.SVY
    Svz = contrainte.SVZ
    Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
    Smt = contrainte.SMT
    ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
    ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);    
    if ratioMax < ratioLimProf:
        fzMax *= 2
    fzCourbe = fzMax/-fyMax*fy + fzMax
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fzCourbe,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzCourbe),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
    );
    TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
    contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
    Sn = contrainte.SN
    Svy = contrainte.SVY
    Svz = contrainte.SVZ
    Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
    Smt = contrainte.SMT
    ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
    ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);    
    if ratioMax > ratioLimProf:
        alpha = 0
        beta = fzCourbe
    else:
        alpha = fzCourbe
        beta = fzMax
    fz = (alpha + beta)/2
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX ={round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fz,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fz**2+fy**2)**0.5,FZ=fz,FY=fy),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
    );
    TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
    contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
    Sn = contrainte.SN
    Svy = contrainte.SVY
    Svz = contrainte.SVZ
    Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
    Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
    Smt = contrainte.SMT
    ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
    ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);
    while abs((ratioLimProf-0.01)-ratioMax) > 0.01:
        if ratioMax < ratioLimProf:
            alpha = fz
        else:
            beta = fz
        fz = (alpha+beta)/2
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fz**2+fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fz,2)}\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fz),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
            MODELE=model,
            CHAM_MATER=material,
            CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            RESULTAT = stat,
            CONTRAINTE = ('SIPO_ELNO',),
        );
        TAB_cont = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='SIPO_ELNO',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
            
        contrainte = TAB_cont.EXTR_TABLE()
        Sn = contrainte.SN
        Svy = contrainte.SVY
        Svz = contrainte.SVZ
        Smfy = contrainte.SMFY
        Smfz = contrainte.SMFZ
        Smt = contrainte.SMT
        ratio = Ratio(value,niveau,Sn, Svy, Svz, Smt, Smfy, Smfz)
        ratioMax = ratio.maxRatio()
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_cont,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_cont,),);
    #-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    ratio.writeOsupFile(curveFile, f*(fz**2+fy**2)**0.5, fy, fz)
    sv.fxCourbeMin.append(fy)
    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fz)
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
sv.timefin = time.time()
print("Temps total = ",sv.timefin-sv.timeInit)
plt.plot(sv.fxCourbeMin,sv.fzCourbeMin)

        dry = torseur.DRY
        drz = torseur.DRZ

            if nbChevilles[i] =='2':                 
                maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
            if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
                maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);
    #-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    osupFile = open(platineFile,"a")
    osupFile.write(f'{round(f*((fz**2+fy**2)**0.5),3)}		{round(fy,3)}		{round(fz,3)}		{round(ratioMax,3)}\n')
    osupFile.close()
    ratioPlatine.append_reaction(dx,dy,dz,drx,dry,drz)
    sv.fxCourbeMin.append(fy)
    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fz)
sv.fxCourbeMin.append(fyMin)
sv.fzCourbeMin.append(0)
osupFile = open(platineFile,"a")
osupFile.write(f'{round(f*-fyMin,3)}		{round(fyMin,3)}    0\n')
osupFile.close()
#----------------------------------QUADRANT 4 FX <0 , FY > 0-------------------------------
for i in range(1,n):
    fy = fyMin/n*(n-i)    
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ=0\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=0),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        FORCE = ('REAC_NODA',),
    );
    TAB_eff = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('encas',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='REAC_NODA',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
    
    torseur = TAB_eff.EXTR_TABLE()
    dx = torseur.DX
    dy = torseur.DY
    dz = torseur.DZ
    drx = torseur.DRX
    dry = torseur.DRY
    drz = torseur.DRZ
     
    nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
    maxRatio = []
    for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
        if nbChevilles[i] =='2':             
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
    ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),); 
    while ratioMax > ratioLimPlat:
        if i ==1:
            fy = (fy + sv.fxCourbeMin[-2])/2
        else:
            fy = (fy + sv.fxCourbeMin[-1])/2
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ=0\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=0),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
            MODELE=model,
            CHAM_MATER=material,
            CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            RESULTAT = stat,
            FORCE = ('REAC_NODA',),
        );
        TAB_eff = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('encas',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='REAC_NODA',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
        torseur = TAB_eff.EXTR_TABLE()
        dx = torseur.DX
        dy = torseur.DY
        dz = torseur.DZ
        drx = torseur.DRX
        dry = torseur.DRY
        drz = torseur.DRZ
         
        nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
        maxRatio = []
        for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
            if nbChevilles[i] =='2':                 
                maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
            if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
                maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fzMax,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzMax),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );
    stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        FORCE = ('REAC_NODA',),
    );
    TAB_eff = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('encas',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='REAC_NODA',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
    
    torseur = TAB_eff.EXTR_TABLE()
    dx = torseur.DX
    dy = torseur.DY
    dz = torseur.DZ
    drx = torseur.DRX
    dry = torseur.DRY
    drz = torseur.DRZ
     
    nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
    maxRatio = []
    for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
        if nbChevilles[i] =='2':             
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))

    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),); 
    if ratioMax < ratioLimPlat:
        fzMax *= 2
    fzCourbe = fzMax/fyMax*fy + fzMax
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fzCourbe,2)}\n')

    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzCourbe),
    );

    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),

    );

        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        FORCE = ('REAC_NODA',),
    );

        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);

    dy = torseur.DY
    dz = torseur.DZ
    drx = torseur.DRX
    dry = torseur.DRY
    drz = torseur.DRZ
     
    nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
    maxRatio = []
    for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
        if nbChevilles[i] =='2':             
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
    ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);    
    if ratioMax > ratioLimPlat:
        alpha = 0
        beta = fzCourbe
    else:
        alpha = fzCourbe
        beta = fzMax
    fz = (alpha + beta)/2
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX ={round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fz,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()
    force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fz**2+fy**2)**0.5,FZ=fz,FY=fy),
    );

    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),

        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);

    dx = torseur.DX
    dy = torseur.DY
    dz = torseur.DZ
    drx = torseur.DRX
    dry = torseur.DRY
    drz = torseur.DRZ
     
    nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
    maxRatio = []
    for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
        if nbChevilles[i] =='2':             
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
    ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);
    while abs((ratioLimPlat-0.01)-ratioMax) > 0.01:
        if ratioMax < 1:
            alpha = fz
        else:
            beta = fz
        fz = (alpha+beta)/2
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fz**2+fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fz,2)}\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fz),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        stat=CALC_CHAMP( reuse =stat,
            MODELE=model,
            CHAM_MATER=material,
            CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            RESULTAT = stat,
            FORCE = ('REAC_NODA',),
        );
        TAB_eff = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('encas',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='REAC_NODA',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
    
        torseur = TAB_eff.EXTR_TABLE()
        dx = torseur.DX
        dy = torseur.DY
        dz = torseur.DZ
        drx = torseur.DRX
        dry = torseur.DRY
        drz = torseur.DRZ
        nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
        maxRatio = []
        for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
            if nbChevilles[i] =='2':                 
                maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
            if nbChevilles[i] =='4':
                maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio4chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);
    #-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
    osupFile = open(platineFile,"a")
    osupFile.write(f'{round(f*((fz**2+fy**2)**0.5),3)}		{round(fy,3)}		{round(fz,3)}		{round(ratioMax,3)}\n')
    osupFile.close()
    ratioPlatine.append_reaction(dx,dy,dz,drx,dry,drz)
    sv.fxCourbeMin.append(fy)
    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fz)

    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);

        fzMax *= 2
    fzCourbe = -fzMax/fyMax*fy + fzMax

    reportFile.close()

    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
        FX = f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzCourbe),
    );
    stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
    EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
            _F(CHARGE=force,),
        ),
    SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
    );

        MODELE=model,
        CHAM_MATER=material,
        CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        RESULTAT = stat,
        FORCE = ('REAC_NODA',),
    );
    TAB_eff = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
	GROUP_NO = ('encas',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='REAC_NODA',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
	TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
	OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
    
    torseur = TAB_eff.EXTR_TABLE()
    dx = torseur.DX
    dy = torseur.DY
    dz = torseur.DZ
    drx = torseur.DRX
    dry = torseur.DRY
    drz = torseur.DRZ
     
    nbChevilles = value['platine']['nbCheville']
    maxRatio = []
    for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
        maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio_flèche(nbCheville, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
    ratioMax = max(maxRatio)
    IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_eff,)
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);  
    if ratioMax > ratioLimPlat:
        alpha = 0
        beta = fzCourbe
    else:
        alpha = fzCourbe
        beta = fzMax
    fz = (alpha + beta)/2
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
    reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
    reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX ={round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ={round(fz,2)}\n')
    reportFile.close()

    FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),

    dy = torseur.DY

    dry = torseur.DRY
    drz = torseur.DRZ

    while abs((ratioLimPlat-0.01)-ratioMax) > 0.01:
        if ratioMax < ratioLimPlat:
            alpha = fz
        else:
            beta = fz
        fz = (alpha+beta)/2

    osupFile = open(rigiditeFile,"a")

    osupFile.close()

    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fz)

        if nbChevilles[i] =='2':                 
            maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio2chevilles(niveau, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
        if nbChevilles[i] =='4':

    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);

    drz = torseur.DRZ

    for i in range(len(nbChevilles)):
        maxRatio.append(ratioPlatine.ratio_flèche(nbCheville, dx, dy, dz, drx, dry, drz,i))
    ratioMax = max(maxRatio)

    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=stat,),);
    DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_eff,),);

            );

                GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
                TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
                OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);            
            depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
            dy = max( depl.DY)
            dz = max( depl.DZ)
            fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
            IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)       
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);        
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);

        osupFile.close()    
        sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fy)
        sv.fyCourbeMin.append(fz)
    osupFile = open(flecheFile,"a")
    osupFile.write(f'{round(f*fyMax,2)}		{round(fyMax,2)}		0\n')
    osupFile.close()
    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fyMax)
    sv.fyCourbeMin.append(0)

    #-------------------------------------QUADRANT 2 fz<0 fx<0 ---------------------------------------------
    #----------------------------- fyMax --------------------------------
    fyMin = -fxMax/f
    reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")

        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        
        TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
        GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
        TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
        OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);    
        depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
        dy = max( depl.DY)
        dz = max( depl.DZ)     
        fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);    
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);
        while abs((fleche_max-0.01)-fleche_adm) > 0.01:
            if fleche_max < fleche_adm:
                alpha = fz
            else:
                beta = fz
            fz = (alpha+beta)/2
            reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
            reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
            reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fz**2+fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fz,2)}\n')
            reportFile.close()
            force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
            FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
                FY=fy,FZ=fz, FX = f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5),
            );
            stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                    _F(CHARGE=force,),
                ),
            SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
            );
            TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
                GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
                TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
                OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);        
            depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
            dy = max( depl.DY)
            dz = max( depl.DZ)     
            fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
            IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);            
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);
        #-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        osupFile = open(flecheFile,"a")
        osupFile.write(f'{round(f*((fy**2+fz**2)**0.5),3)}		{round(fy,3)}		{round(fz,3)}		{round(ratioMax,3)}\n')
        osupFile.close()    
        sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fy)
        sv.fyCourbeMin.append(fz)
    osupFile = open(flecheFile,"a")
    osupFile.write(f'{round(f*fyMin ,3)}		{round(fyMin ,3)}		0		\n')
    osupFile.close()
    sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fyMin)
    sv.fyCourbeMin.append(0)
    #----------------------------------QUADRANT 4 fz <0 , fx > 0-------------------------------
    for i in range(1,n):
        fy = fyMin/n*(n-i)    
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = 0\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2)**0.5,FY=fy),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        
        TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
        depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
        dy = max( depl.DY)
        dz = max( depl.DZ)     
        fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);        
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),); 
        while fleche_max > fleche_adm:
            if i ==1:
                fy = (fy + sv.fzCourbeMin[-2])/2
            else:
                fy = (fy + sv.fzCourbeMin[-1])/2
            reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
            reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
            reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = 0\n')
            reportFile.close()
            force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
            FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
                FX = f*(fy**2)**0.5,FY=fy),
            );
            stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                    _F(CHARGE=force,),
                ),
            SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
            );
            TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
                GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
                TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
                OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);        
            depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
            dy = max( depl.DY)
            dz = max( depl.DZ)     
            fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
            IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);        
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fzMax,2)}\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2+fzMax**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzMax),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        
        TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);    
        depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
        dy = max( depl.DY)
        dz = max( depl.DZ)     
        fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);    
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),); 
        if fleche_max < fleche_adm:
            fzMax *= 2
        fzCourbe = fzMax/-fyMax*fy + fzMax
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fzCourbe,2)}\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2+fzCourbe**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fzCourbe),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        
        TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);    
        depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
        dy = max( depl.DY)
        dz = max( depl.DZ)     
        fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);    
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);    
        if fleche_max > fleche_adm:
            alpha = 0
            beta = fzCourbe
        else:
            alpha = fzCourbe
            beta = fzMax
        fz = (alpha + beta)/2
        reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
        reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
        reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fz,2)}\n')
        reportFile.close()
        force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
        FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
            FX = f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,FY=fy,FZ=fz),
        );
        stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
        EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                _F(CHARGE=force,),
            ),
        SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
        );
        
        TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
            GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
            TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
            OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);    
        depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
        dy = max( depl.DY)
        dz = max( depl.DZ)     
        fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
        IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);    
        DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);
        while abs((fleche_max - 0.01) - fleche_adm) > 0.01:
            if fleche_max < fleche_adm:
                alpha = fz
            else:
                beta = fz
            fz = (alpha+beta)/2
            reportFile = open(resultfile,"a")
            reportFile.write(f'{dash}\n')
            reportFile.write(f'CHARGEMENT: FX = {round(f*(fy**2+fz**2)**0.5,2)}, FY = {round(fy,2)}, FZ = {round(fz,2)}\n')
            reportFile.close()
            force=AFFE_CHAR_MECA(MODELE=model,
            FORCE_NODALE=_F(GROUP_NO=('load',),
                FX = f*(fy**2+fy**2)**0.5,FZ=fz,FY=fy),
            );
            stat=MECA_STATIQUE(MODELE=model,CHAM_MATER=material,CARA_ELEM=elemcar,
            EXCIT=(			_F(CHARGE=encast,),
                    _F(CHARGE=force,),
                ),
            SOLVEUR=_F(RESI_RELA=1.E-04,NPREC=11,),
            );
            TAB_depl = POST_RELEVE_T(ACTION=_F(INTITULE='sum reactions',
                GROUP_NO = ('ALL',),RESULTAT=stat,NOM_CHAM='DEPL',TOUT_CMP='OUI',
                TOUT_ORDRE='OUI',
                OPERATION='EXTRACTION',),);
        
            depl = TAB_depl.EXTR_TABLE()
            dy = max( depl.DY)
            dz = max( depl.DZ)     
            fleche_max = max(dy, dz)
            IMPR_TABLE (TABLE=TAB_depl,)
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=force,),);        
            DETRUIRE(CONCEPT=_F(NOM=TAB_depl,),);
        #-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
        osupFile = open(flecheFile,"a")
        osupFile.write(f'{round(f*((fy**2+fz**2)**0.5),3)}		{round(fy,3)}		{round(fz,3)}		{round(ratioMax,3)}\n')
        osupFile.close()    
        sv.fzCourbeMin.append(fy)
        sv.fyCourbeMin.append(fz)
    import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
    sv.timefin = time.time()
    print("Temps total = ",sv.timefin-sv.timeInit)
    plt.plot(sv.fzCourbeMin,sv.fyCourbeMin) 
    plt.show()
    osupFile = open(flecheFile,"a")
    osupFile.write(f'{round(f*fzMax_init,2)}		0		{round(fzMax_init,2)}\n')
    osupFile.close()     
FIN()
